### Remark 18.1.3 Computation of the identity type of `dependent-cocone`

Before we state the main theorem of this section, we also state a dependent
version of the pullback property of pushouts.

## Theorem 18.1.4

    The following properties are all equivalent:

    1. universal-property-pushout
    2. pullback-property-pushout
    3. dependent-pullback-property-pushout
    4. dependent-universal-property-pushout
    5. Ind-pushout

We have already shown (1) ↔ (2). Therefore we will first show (3) ↔ (4) ↔ (5).
Finally, we will show (2) ↔ (3). Here are the precise references to the proofs
of those parts:

- Proof of (1) → (2): `pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout`
- Proof of (2) → (1): `universal-property-pushout-pullback-property-pushout`
- Proof of (2) → (3): `dependent-pullback-property-pullback-property-pushout`
- Proof of (3) → (2): `pullback-property-dependent-pullback-property-pushout`
- Proof of (3) → (4):
  `dependent-universal-property-dependent-pullback-property-pushout`
- Proof of (4) → (3):
  `dependent-pullback-property-dependent-universal-property-pushout`
- Proof of (4) → (5): `Ind-pushout-dependent-universal-property-pushout`
- Proof of (5) → (4): `dependent-universal-property-pushout-Ind-pushout`

### Proof of Theorem 18.1.4, (3) implies (2)

              <a id="4075" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4077" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="4085" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="4088" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="4090" class="Symbol">→</a>

                  <a id="4151" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4153" href="foundation.constant-type-families.html#1824" class="Function">tr-constant-type-family</a> <a id="4177" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4178" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4180" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4181" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4184" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4187" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3582" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="4189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4190" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3572" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="4192" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4193" class="Symbol">))))</a>
                  <a id="4216" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4218" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="4221" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4224" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4226" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4227" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="4248" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4250" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-dependent-functions.html#1181" class="Function">apd</a> <a id="4254" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4257" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4259" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4260" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="4281" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4283" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="4287" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4288" href="foundation.constant-type-families.html#2113" class="Function">apd-constant-type-family</a> <a id="4313" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4315" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4316" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4318" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4088" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4319" class="Symbol">))))))</a> <a id="4326" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
            <a id="4340" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4342" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#9325" class="Function">eq-htpy-concat-htpy</a>
              <a id="4376" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4378" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="4380" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4380" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="4382" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4384" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="4388" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4389" href="foundation.constant-type-families.html#1824" class="Function">tr-constant-type-family</a> <a id="4413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4414" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4416" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4380" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4417" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4419" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4420" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4423" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3582" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="4425" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4426" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3572" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="4428" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4380" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4429" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="4449" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4451" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="4453" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4453" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="4455" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4457" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-dependent-functions.html#1181" class="Function">apd</a> <a id="4461" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4019" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4464" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3592" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="4466" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4453" class="Bound">s</a><a id="4467" class="Symbol">)))))))</a>
    <a id="4479" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4481" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3596" class="Bound">dpb</a> <a id="4485" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="4488" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4488" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4492" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#3600" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="4493" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Proof of Theorem 18.1.4, (2) implies (3)

We first define the family of lifts, which is indexed by maps $Y → X$.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="fam-lifts"></a><a id="4627" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4627" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="4637" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="6024" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1881" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="6027" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6029" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5560" class="Function">tr-eq-htpy-fam-lifts</a> <a id="6050" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5973" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6052" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5995" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6055" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2970" class="Function">refl-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="6066" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6007" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6067" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="6078" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6080" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5264" class="Function">tr-eq-htpy-fam-lifts-refl-htpy</a> <a id="6111" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5973" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6113" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5995" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6115" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6007" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6116" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6120" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5879" class="Function">compute-tr-eq-htpy-fam-lifts</a> <a id="6149" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6149" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6151" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6151" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6153" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6153" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6155" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6161" href="foundation.homotopy-induction.html#4514" class="Function">compute-ind-htpy</a> <a id="6178" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6153" class="Bound">f</a>
      <a id="6186" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6188" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6190" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6190" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6192" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6192" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="6194" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6196" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5006" class="Function">TR-EQ-HTPY-FAM-LIFTS</a> <a id="6217" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6149" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6219" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6151" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6221" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6192" class="Bound">H</a><a id="6222" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="6230" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6232" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#5264" class="Function">tr-eq-htpy-fam-lifts-refl-htpy</a> <a id="6263" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6149" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6265" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6151" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6267" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6153" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6268" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
One of the basic operations on lifts is precomposition by an ordinary function.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="precompose-lifts"></a><a id="6364" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="6381" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6385" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6386" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6386" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="6389" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6389" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="6392" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6392" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="6395" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6395" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="6398" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6400" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6405" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6407" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6408" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6408" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6412" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6415" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6386" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="6417" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6419" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6420" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6420" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6424" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6427" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6389" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="6429" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6431" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6432" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6432" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6434" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6436" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6439" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6392" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="6441" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="6445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6446" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6446" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6448" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6450" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6432" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6452" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6454" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6457" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6395" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="6459" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6464" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6464" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6468" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6408" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6470" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6472" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6420" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6473" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6475" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6478" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6478" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6482" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6420" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6486" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6432" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6489" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="6493" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6494" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4627" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="6504" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6420" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6506" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6446" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6508" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6478" class="Bound">h</a><a id="6509" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6511" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6514" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4627" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="6524" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6408" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6526" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6446" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6529" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6478" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6531" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="6533" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6464" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6534" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="6537" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="6554" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6554" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6556" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6556" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6558" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6558" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6560" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6560" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="6563" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6563" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="6565" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6567" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6560" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="6570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6571" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6556" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6573" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6563" class="Bound">a</a><a id="6574" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Given two homotopic maps, their precomposition functions have different
codomains. However, there is a commuting triangle. We obtain this triangle by
homotopy induction.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="TRIANGLE-PRECOMPOSE-LIFTS"></a><a id="6760" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6760" class="Function">TRIANGLE-PRECOMPOSE-LIFTS</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6790" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="6792" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6792" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="6795" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6795" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="6798" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6798" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="6801" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6801" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="6804" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6806" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6814" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6814" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6816" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6818" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6821" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6792" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="6823" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6825" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6826" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6826" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6830" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6833" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6795" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="6835" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6837" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6838" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6838" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6842" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6845" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6798" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="6847" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="6851" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6853" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6853" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6855" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6857" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6869" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6871" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6871" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6873" class="Symbol">:</a> <a class="Bound">B</a><a id="6880" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6883" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6883" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="6885" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6899" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6900" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6792" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="6903" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" <a id="6919" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6760" class="Function">TRIANGLE-PRECOMPOSE-LIFTS</a> <a id="6945" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6946" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="6948" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6950" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6950" class="Bound">A</a><a id="6951" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6953" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6954" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6954" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6955" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6957" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6958" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6958" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6959" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6961" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6961" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="6963" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6964" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6964" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6965" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6967" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6968" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6968" class="Bound">g</a><a id="6969" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6971" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6971" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="6973" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="6977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6978" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6978" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6982" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6954" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6984" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6986" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6958" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6987" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6989" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="6995" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6997" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6998" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications.html#832" class="Function">tr</a> <a id="7001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7002" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4627" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="7012" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6950" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7014" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6961" class="Bound">P</a><a id="7015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7018" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="7026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7027" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6978" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="7029" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="7032" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6971" class="Bound">H</a><a id="7033" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="7037" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="7039" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7040" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="7057" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6961" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7059" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6964" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7061" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6978" class="Bound">h</a><a id="7062" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7065" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a>
    <a id="7071" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7073" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="7090" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6961" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7092" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6968" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7094" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6978" class="Bound">h</a><a id="7095" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="triangle-precompose-lifts-refl-htpy"></a><a id="7098" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7098" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts-refl-htpy</a> <a id="7134" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7138" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7139" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7139" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="7142" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7142" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="7145" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7145" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="7148" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7148" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="7151" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7153" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="7158" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7160" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7161" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7161" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7163" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7165" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7168" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7139" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="7170" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7172" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7173" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7173" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7175" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7177" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7180" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7142" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="7182" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7185" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7185" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7187" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7189" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7192" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7145" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="7194" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="7198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7199" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7199" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7203" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7185" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7205" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7207" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7210" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7148" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="7212" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7214" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7215" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7215" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7217" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7219" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7161" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7221" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7223" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7173" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7224" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7228" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6760" class="Function">TRIANGLE-PRECOMPOSE-LIFTS</a> <a id="7254" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7199" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7257" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2970" class="Function">refl-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="7268" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7215" class="Bound">f</a><a id="7269" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7271" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7098" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts-refl-htpy</a> <a id="7307" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7308" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="7310" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7312" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7312" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7313" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7315" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7315" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7317" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7317" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7319" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7319" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="7321" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7321" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="7324" class="Symbol">=</a>

  <a id="7827" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1881" class="Datatype">Id</a>
    <a id="7834" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7836" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7383" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts</a> <a id="7862" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7796" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7865" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2970" class="Function">refl-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="7876" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7812" class="Bound">f</a><a id="7877" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7969" href="foundation.homotopy-induction.html#4514" class="Function">compute-ind-htpy</a> <a id="7986" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7963" class="Bound">f</a>
    <a id="7992" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7994" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="7996" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7996" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7998" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8000" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6760" class="Function">TRIANGLE-PRECOMPOSE-LIFTS</a> <a id="8026" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7961" class="Bound">P</a><a id="8027" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="8033" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8035" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7098" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts-refl-htpy</a> <a id="8071" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7961" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8073" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7963" class="Bound">f</a><a id="8074" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
There is a similar commuting triangle with the computed transport function. This
time we don't use homotopy induction to construct the homotopy. We give an
explicit definition instead.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;"></a><a id="8275" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8275" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8302" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="8366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8367" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8367" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8369" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8371" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8353" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8373" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8375" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8378" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8316" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="8380" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8382" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8383" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8383" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8385" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8385" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8387" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8389" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8329" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8391" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8393" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8341" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8394" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8397" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8397" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="8399" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8401" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8383" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8403" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="8405" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8385" class="Bound">g</a><a id="8406" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8408" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8410" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8411" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8411" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8415" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8341" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8417" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8419" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8353" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8420" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8422" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="8426" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8428" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8429" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4764" class="Function">tr-fam-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8443" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8367" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8445" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8411" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8447" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8397" class="Bound">H</a><a id="8448" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8450" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8453" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="8470" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8367" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8472" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8383" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8474" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8411" class="Bound">h</a><a id="8475" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8478" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a>

<a id="8508" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8275" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8535" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8535" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8537" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8537" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="8539" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8539" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8541" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8541" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8543" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8545" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="8553" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8556" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8556" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8558" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8560" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-dependent-functions.html#1181" class="Function">apd</a> <a id="8564" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8541" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8567" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8537" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="8569" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8556" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8570" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="compute-triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;"></a><a id="8574" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8574" class="Function">compute-triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8609" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8613" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8614" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8614" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="8617" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8617" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="8620" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8620" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="8623" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8623" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="8626" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8628" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8633" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8635" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8636" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8636" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8638" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8640" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8643" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8614" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="8645" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8647" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8648" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8648" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8650" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8652" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8655" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8617" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="8657" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8660" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8662" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8664" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8667" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8620" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="8669" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8674" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8674" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8676" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8678" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8660" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8680" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8682" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8685" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8623" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="8687" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8690" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8690" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8692" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8694" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8636" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8696" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8698" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8648" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8699" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8701" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8703" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8704" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8704" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8706" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8708" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8648" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8710" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8712" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8660" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8713" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8715" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="8719" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8721" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8275" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8748" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8674" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8751" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2970" class="Function">refl-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="8762" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8690" class="Bound">f</a><a id="8763" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8765" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8704" class="Bound">h</a><a id="8766" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8768" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a>
  <a id="8772" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8774" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2970" class="Function">refl-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="8785" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8787" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="8804" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8674" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8806" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8690" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8808" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8704" class="Bound">h</a><a id="8809" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="8812" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8574" class="Function">compute-triangle-precompose-lifts&#39;</a> <a id="8847" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8847" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="8849" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8849" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8851" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8851" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="8853" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#8853" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8855" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8857" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3630" class="Function">eq-htpy-refl-htpy</a> <a id="8875" class="Symbol">_</a>
</pre>
There is a coherence between the two commuting triangles. This coherence is
again constructed by homotopy induction.

  <a id="11556" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#862" class="Function">coherence-square-maps</a>
    <a id="11582" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11584" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11143" class="Function">precompose-total-lifts</a> <a id="11607" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11525" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11609" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11541" class="Bound">f</a><a id="11610" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="11616" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11618" href="foundation-core.type-theoretic-principle-of-choice.html#2049" class="Function">map-inv-distributive-Π-Σ</a> <a id="11643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11644" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="11646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11648" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11499" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11649" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11651" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11652" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="11654" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11656" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11658" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11658" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11660" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11662" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11511" class="Bound">X</a><a id="11663" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11665" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11666" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="11668" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11670" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11672" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11672" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11674" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11674" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="11676" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11678" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11525" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11680" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11674" class="Bound">y</a><a id="11681" class="Symbol">})</a>
    <a id="11688" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11690" href="foundation-core.type-theoretic-principle-of-choice.html#2049" class="Function">map-inv-distributive-Π-Σ</a><a id="11714" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="11720" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11722" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11724" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11724" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="11726" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11728" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11724" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="11730" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="11732" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11541" class="Bound">f</a><a id="11733" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11735" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11418" class="Function">coherence-square-map-inv-distributive-Π-Σ</a> <a id="11777" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11777" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11779" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11779" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11783" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2906" class="Function">refl-htpy</a>
</pre>
Our goal is now to produce a homotopy between `precompose-total-lifts P f` and
`precompose-total-lifts P g` for homotopic maps `f` and `g`, and a coherence
filling a cylinder.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="HTPY-PRECOMPOSE-TOTAL-LIFTS"></a><a id="11983" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11983" class="Function">HTPY-PRECOMPOSE-TOTAL-LIFTS</a> <a id="12011" class="Symbol">:</a>

href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12288" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="12337" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12339" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12340" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12340" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12342" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12344" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12328" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="12346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12348" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="12351" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12291" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="12353" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12357" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12358" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12358" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12360" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12360" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12362" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12364" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12304" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12366" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12368" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12316" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12369" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12372" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12372" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="12374" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12376" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12358" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12378" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="12380" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12360" class="Bound">g</a><a id="12381" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12383" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12385" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#11983" class="Function">HTPY-PRECOMPOSE-TOTAL-LIFTS</a> <a id="12413" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12340" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12415" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12372" class="Bound">H</a>
<a id="12417" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12249" class="Function">htpy-precompose-total-lifts</a> <a id="12445" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12446" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="12448" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12450" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12450" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12451" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12453" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12454" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12454" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12457" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12457" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12459" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12460" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12460" class="Bound">f</a><a id="12461" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12463" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12464" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12464" class="Bound">g</a><a id="12465" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12467" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12467" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="12469" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12473" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.html#2488" class="Function">htpy-map-Σ</a>
    <a id="12488" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12490" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#4627" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="12500" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12450" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12502" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12457" class="Bound">P</a><a id="12503" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12509" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12511" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="12513" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12513" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="12515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12517" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="12525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12526" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12513" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="12528" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="12531" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12467" class="Bound">H</a><a id="12532" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="12539" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12541" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#6364" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="12558" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12457" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12560" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12460" class="Bound">f</a><a id="12561" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12567" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12569" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#7383" class="Function">triangle-precompose-lifts</a> <a id="12595" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12457" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="12597" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#12467" class="Bound">H</a><a id="12598" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We show that when `htpy-precompose-total-lifts` is applied to `refl-htpy`, it
computes to `refl-htpy`.

        <a id="18467" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18469" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#5353" class="Function">right-unit-htpy</a> <a id="18485" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3281" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="18488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18489" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#10136" class="Function">coherence-triangle-precompose-lifts</a> <a id="18525" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18048" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="18527" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18033" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="18529" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a><a id="18531" class="Symbol">))))</a>
    <a id="18540" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18542" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#15817" class="Function">is-pullback-cone-family-dependent-pullback-property</a> <a id="18594" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18013" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18596" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18015" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18598" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18058" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18600" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18037" class="Bound">pullback-c</a> <a id="18611" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18048" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="18613" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a><a id="18615" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
This concludes the proof of Theorem 18.1.4.

We give some further useful implications.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="dependent-universal-property-universal-property-pushout"></a><a id="18718" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18718" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="18774" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="18778" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="18780" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18780" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="18783" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18783" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="18786" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18786" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="18789" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18789" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="18792" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18794" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="18799" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18801" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18802" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18802" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="18804" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18806" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18809" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18780" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="18811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18814" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18814" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18816" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18818" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18821" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18783" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="18823" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18825" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18826" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18826" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18830" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18833" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18786" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="18835" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18837" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18838" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18838" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="18840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18842" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="18845" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18789" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="18847" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="18851" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18853" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18853" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18855" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18857" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18802" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="18859" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18861" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18814" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18862" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18865" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18865" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18869" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18802" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="18871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18873" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18826" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18874" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18876" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18877" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18877" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18879" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18881" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1443" class="Function">cocone</a> <a id="18888" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18853" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18890" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18865" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18892" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18838" class="Bound">X</a><a id="18893" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18895" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="18899" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18901" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18902" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18902" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="18904" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18906" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="18911" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18913" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18915" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#2873" class="Function">universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="18942" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18902" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="18944" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18853" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18946" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18865" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18948" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18877" class="Bound">c</a><a id="18949" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18951" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="18955" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18957" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18958" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18958" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="18960" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18962" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="18967" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18969" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18971" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.dependent-universal-property-pushouts.html#1585" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="19008" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18958" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19010" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18853" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19012" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18865" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19014" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18877" class="Bound">c</a><a id="19015" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="19017" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18718" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="19073" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19073" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19075" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19075" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19077" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19077" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19079" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19079" class="Bound">up-X</a> <a id="19084" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="19088" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.dependent-universal-property-pushouts.html#7849" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-dependent-pullback-property-pushout</a> <a id="19153" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19073" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19155" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19075" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19157" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19077" class="Bound">c</a>
    <a id="19163" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19165" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#17644" class="Function">dependent-pullback-property-pullback-property-pushout</a> <a id="19219" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19073" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19221" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19075" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19223" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19077" class="Bound">c</a>
      <a id="19231" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19233" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#9281" class="Function">pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="19286" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19073" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19288" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19075" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19290" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19077" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19292" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19079" class="Bound">up-X</a><a id="19296" class="Symbol">))</a>

## Section 16.2 Families over pushouts

### Definition 18.2.1

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fam-pushout"></a><a id="19375" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="19387" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="19391" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19392" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19392" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="19395" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19395" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="19398" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19398" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="19401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19403" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="19408" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19410" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19411" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19411" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19415" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="19420" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19422" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19423" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19423" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19425" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19427" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19430" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19392" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="19432" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19435" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19435" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19439" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19442" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19395" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="19444" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19446" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19447" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19447" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="19449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19451" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19454" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19398" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="19456" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="19460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19461" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19461" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19463" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19465" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19423" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19467" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19469" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19435" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19470" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19472" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19473" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19473" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19475" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19477" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19423" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19479" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19481" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19447" class="Bound">B</a><a id="19482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19486" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19489" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19490" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19392" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="19493" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="19495" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19395" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="19498" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="19500" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19398" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="19503" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="19505" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="19510" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19411" class="Bound">l</a><a id="19511" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="19513" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="19525" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19525" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19528" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19528" class="Bound">S</a><a id="19529" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19531" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19532" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19532" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19533" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19535" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19536" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19536" class="Bound">B</a><a id="19537" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19539" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19539" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19541" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19541" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19543" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="19547" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#505" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="19549" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19551" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19532" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19553" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19555" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19558" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19525" class="Bound">l</a><a id="19559" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="19565" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19567" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="19569" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19569" class="Bound">PA</a> <a id="19572" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19574" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#505" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="19576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19577" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19536" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="19579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19581" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19584" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19525" class="Bound">l</a><a id="19585" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="19593" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19595" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="19597" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19597" class="Bound">PB</a> <a id="19600" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19602" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19603" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19603" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="19605" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19607" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19528" class="Bound">S</a><a id="19608" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19612" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19569" class="Bound">PA</a> <a id="19615" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19616" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19539" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19618" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19603" class="Bound">s</a><a id="19619" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19621" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2669" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="19623" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19597" class="Bound">PB</a> <a id="19626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19627" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19541" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="19629" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19603" class="Bound">s</a><a id="19630" class="Symbol">)))</a>

### Characterizing the identity type of `Fam-pushout`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="coherence-equiv-Fam-pushout"></a><a id="19702" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19702" class="Function">coherence-equiv-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="19730" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="19734" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="19736" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19736" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="19739" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19739" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="19742" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19742" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="19745" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19745" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19747" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19747" class="Bound">l&#39;</a> <a id="19750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19752" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="19757" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19759" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19760" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19760" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19762" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19764" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19767" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19736" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="19769" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19771" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19772" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19772" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19776" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19779" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19739" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="19781" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19783" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19784" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19784" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="19786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19788" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="19791" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19742" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="19793" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="19824" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19826" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19826" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="19828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19830" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="19842" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19745" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19844" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19799" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19846" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19811" class="Bound">g</a><a id="19847" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19849" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19850" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19850" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="19852" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19854" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="19866" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19747" class="Bound">l&#39;</a> <a id="19869" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19799" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19871" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19811" class="Bound">g</a><a id="19872" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19874" class="Symbol">→</a>

  <a id="23033" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23034" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23034" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23036" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23038" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#22996" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23040" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23042" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23008" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23043" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23045" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23046" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23046" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="23048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23050" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#22996" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23052" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23054" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23020" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23055" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23057" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23058" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23058" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23060" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23060" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="23062" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23064" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="23076" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#22984" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="23078" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23034" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23080" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23046" class="Bound">g</a><a id="23081" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23083" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="23087" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23089" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23091" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#22323" class="Function">eq-equiv-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="23112" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23113" class="Argument">P</a> <a id="23115" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23117" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23058" class="Bound">P</a><a id="23118" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23120" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23121" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23060" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="23122" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="23125" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a>
    <a id="23131" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23133" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20873" class="Function">equiv-Fam-pushout-eq</a> <a id="23154" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23155" class="Argument">P</a> <a id="23157" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23159" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23058" class="Bound">P</a><a id="23160" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23162" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23163" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23060" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="23164" class="Symbol">}))</a> <a id="23168" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="23170" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a>
<a id="23173" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#22935" class="Function">is-retraction-eq-equiv-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="23208" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23209" class="Argument">P</a> <a id="23211" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23213" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23213" class="Bound">P</a><a id="23214" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23216" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23217" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23217" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="23218" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23220" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="23224" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#6908" class="Function">is-retraction-map-inv-is-equiv</a> <a id="23255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23256" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#21707" class="Function">is-equiv-equiv-Fam-pushout-eq</a> <a id="23286" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23213" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23288" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23217" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="23289" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
This concludes the characterization of the identity type of `Fam-pushout`.

### Definition 18.2.2

<pre class="Agda"><a id="desc-fam"></a><a id="23403" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23403" class="Function">desc-fam</a> <a id="23412" class="Symbol">:</a>

      <a id="23657" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23659" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="23661" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23661" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="23663" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23666" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#586" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="23671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23672" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications.html#832" class="Function">tr</a> <a id="23675" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23583" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23678" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23683" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23687" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23581" class="Bound">c</a><a id="23688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23690" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23661" class="Bound">s</a><a id="23691" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23695" href="foundation.transport-along-identifications.html#1277" class="Function">is-equiv-tr</a> <a id="23707" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23583" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="23709" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23710" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23714" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23715" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23719" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23581" class="Bound">c</a><a id="23720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23722" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23661" class="Bound">s</a><a id="23723" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
</pre>
### Theorem 18.2.3

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fam-pushout-cocone-UU"></a><a id="23762" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23762" class="Function">Fam-pushout-cocone-UU</a> <a id="23784" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="23788" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23789" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23789" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="23792" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23792" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="23795" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23795" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="23798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23800" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="23805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23808" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23808" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="23810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23812" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="23817" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23819" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23820" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23820" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23822" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23824" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="23827" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23789" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="23829" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23832" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23832" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23836" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="23839" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23792" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="23841" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23843" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23844" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23844" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23848" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="23851" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23795" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="23853" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="23857" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23858" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23858" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23860" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23862" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23820" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23864" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23866" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23832" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23867" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23869" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23870" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23870" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="23872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23874" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23820" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23876" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23878" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23844" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23879" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23881" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23883" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1443" class="Function">cocone</a> <a id="23890" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23858" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23892" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23870" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="23894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23895" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="23898" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23808" class="Bound">l</a><a id="23899" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23901" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23903" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="23915" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23808" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="23917" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23858" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23919" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23870" class="Bound">g</a>
<a id="23921" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23762" class="Function">Fam-pushout-cocone-UU</a> <a id="23943" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23943" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="23945" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="23949" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.html#1478" class="Function">tot</a> <a id="23953" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="23956" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23956" class="Bound">PA</a> <a id="23959" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23962" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.html#1478" class="Function">tot</a> <a id="23966" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="23969" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23969" class="Bound">PB</a> <a id="23972" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23972" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="23974" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23974" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="23976" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23978" href="foundation-core.univalence.html#855" class="Function">equiv-eq</a> <a id="23987" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23988" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23972" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="23990" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23974" class="Bound">s</a><a id="23991" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="is-equiv-Fam-pushout-cocone-UU"></a><a id="23997" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#23997" class="Function">is-equiv-Fam-pushout-cocone-UU</a> <a id="24028" class="Symbol">:</a>

### Corollary 18.2.4
