  <a id="28200" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="28202" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28202" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28204" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28206" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28151" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="28208" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28210" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28163" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28214" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="28216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28218" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28151" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="28220" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28222" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28175" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28223" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28225" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28226" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="28228" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28230" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1443" class="Function">cocone</a> <a id="28237" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28202" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28239" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="28241" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28187" class="Bound">X</a><a id="28242" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28244" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="28248" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28250" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28250" class="Bound">up-X</a> <a id="28255" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28257" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28258" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28258" class="Bound">l&#39;</a> <a id="28261" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28263" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="28268" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28270" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28272" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#2873" class="Function">universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="28299" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28258" class="Bound">l&#39;</a> <a id="28302" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28202" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28304" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="28306" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a><a id="28307" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28309" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="28313" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28315" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28315" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28317" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28319" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#19375" class="Function">Fam-pushout</a> <a id="28331" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28139" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="28333" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28202" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28335" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28214" class="Bound">g</a><a id="28336" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28338" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="28342" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28344" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28344" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="28346" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28348" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28151" class="Bound">S</a><a id="28349" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28351" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="28357" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28359" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28361" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2869" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="28371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28372" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#27650" class="Function">compute-right-fam-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="28402" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="28404" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28250" class="Bound">up-X</a> <a id="28409" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28315" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28412" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28214" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="28414" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28344" class="Bound">s</a><a id="28415" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28419" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a>
      <a id="28427" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28429" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2869" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="28439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28440" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28444" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28445" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28449" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28315" class="Bound">P</a><a id="28450" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28452" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28344" class="Bound">s</a><a id="28453" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28457" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a>
    <a id="28463" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28465" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28467" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications.html#832" class="Function">tr</a> <a id="28470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28471" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#26490" class="Function">fam-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="28487" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="28489" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28250" class="Bound">up-X</a> <a id="28494" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28315" class="Bound">P</a><a id="28495" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28497" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28498" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28503" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28507" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a><a id="28508" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28510" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28344" class="Bound">s</a><a id="28511" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28514" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a>
      <a id="28522" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28524" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2869" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="28534" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28535" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#27228" class="Function">compute-left-fam-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="28564" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28226" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="28566" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28250" class="Bound">up-X</a> <a id="28571" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28315" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28573" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28574" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28202" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28576" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#28344" class="Bound">s</a><a id="28577" class="Symbol">))))</a>

## Section 18.3 The Flattening lemma for pushouts

### Definition 18.3.1

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28786" class="Comment">{-
cocone-flattening-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  { S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  ( f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X)
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  cocone
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( Σ X Q)
cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e =
  pair
    ( map-Σ Q
      ( pr1 c)
      ( λ a → map-equiv (pr1 e a)))
    ( pair
      ( map-Σ Q
        ( pr1 (pr2 c))
        ( λ b → map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) b)))
      ( htpy-map-Σ Q
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → map-equiv (pr1 e (f s)))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s))))
-}</a>
</pre>
### Theorem 18.3.2 The flattening lemma

<pre class="Agda"><a id="29550" class="Comment">{-
coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; :
  {l1 l2 l3 : Level} {B : UU l1} {Q : B → UU l2} {T : UU l3}
  {b b&#39; : B} (α : Id b b&#39;) {y : Q b} {y&#39; : Q b&#39;} (β : Id (tr Q α y) y&#39;)
  (h : (b : B) → Q b → T) → Id (h b y) (h b&#39; y&#39;)
coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; refl refl h = refl

coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {P : A → UU l3} {Q : B → UU l4} {T : UU l5}
  {f f&#39; : A → B} (H : f ~ f&#39;)
  {g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)}
  {g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a)}
  (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a))
  (h : (b : B) → Q b → T) → (a : A) (p : P a) →
  Id (h (f a) (g a p)) (h (f&#39; a) (g&#39; a p))
coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H K h a p =
  coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; (H a) (K a p) h
coherence-cube-flattening-lemma :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {P : A → UU l3} {Q : B → UU l4} {T : UU l5}
  {f f&#39; : A → B} (H : f ~ f&#39;)
  {g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)}
  {g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a)}
  (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a))
  (h : Σ B Q → T) →
  Id ( eq-htpy
       ( λ a → eq-htpy
         ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H K (ev-pair h) a)))
     ( ap ev-pair
       ( htpy-precomp (htpy-map-Σ Q H g K) T h))
coherence-cube-flattening-lemma
  {A = A} {B} {P} {Q} {T} {f = f} {f&#39;} H {g} {g&#39;} K =
  ind-htpy f
    ( λ f&#39; H&#39; →
      (g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)) (g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a))
      (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H&#39; a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a)) (h : Σ B Q → T) →
      Id ( eq-htpy
           ( λ a → eq-htpy
             ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H&#39; K (ev-pair h) a)))
         ( ap ev-pair
           ( htpy-precomp (htpy-map-Σ Q H&#39; g K) T h)))
    ( λ g g&#39; K h → {!ind-htpy g (λ g&#39; K&#39; → (h : Σ B Q → T) →
      Id ( eq-htpy
           ( λ a → eq-htpy
             ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma
                refl-htpy (λ a → htpy-eq (K&#39; a)) (ev-pair h) a)))
         ( ap ev-pair
           ( htpy-precomp
              ( htpy-map-Σ Q refl-htpy g
                (λ a → htpy-eq (K&#39; a))) T h))) ? (λ a → eq-htpy (K a)) h!})
    H g g&#39; K

flattening-pushout&#39; :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  (f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  (l : Level) →
  pullback-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
flattening-pushout&#39; f g c P Q e l T =
  is-pullback-top-is-pullback-bottom-cube-is-equiv
    ( ( map-Π (λ x → precomp-Π (map-equiv (pr1 e x)) (λ q → T))) ∘
      ( precomp-Π (pr1 c) (λ x → (Q x) → T)))
    ( ( map-Π (λ x → precomp-Π (map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) x)) (λ q → T))) ∘
      ( precomp-Π (pr1 (pr2 c)) (λ x → (Q x) → T)))
    ( precomp-Π f (λ a → (pr1 P a) → T))
    ( ( map-Π (λ s → precomp (map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)) T)) ∘
      ( precomp-Π g (λ b → (pr1 (pr2 P) b) → T)))
    ( precomp (map-Σ Q (pr1 c) (λ a → map-equiv (pr1 e a))) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ Q (pr1 (pr2 c)) (λ b → map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) b))) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id)) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s))) T)
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ( htpy-precomp
      ( htpy-map-Σ Q
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → map-equiv (pr1 e (f s)))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s)))
      ( T))
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    ( λ h → eq-htpy (λ s → eq-htpy
      ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s))
        ( h)
        ( s))))
    {!!}
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    {!!}

flattening-pushout :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  (f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  (l : Level) →
  universal-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
flattening-pushout f g c P Q e l =
  universal-property-pushout-pullback-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
    ( flattening-pushout&#39; f g c P Q e l)
-}</a>
</pre>
